HELP_REGEX_SYNTAX_MENU = "&Regular Expression Syntax"
HELP_REGEX_SYNTAX_MENU_HELP = "Show regular expression syntax help."

HELP_REGEX_SYNTAX_CAPTION = "Regular Expression Syntax - Everything"

HELP_REGEX_SYNTAX_TEXT = "\r\n"
	"Regular Expression Syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"a|b\tMatches a or b\r\n"
	"gr(a|e)y\tMatches gray or grey\r\n"
	".\tMatches any single character\r\n"
	"[abc]\tMatches a single character a, b or c\r\n"
	"[^abc]\tMatches any single character except a, b or c\r\n"
	"[a-z]\tMatches a single character in the range a to z\r\n"
	"[a-zA-Z]\tMatches a single character in the range a to z or A to Z\r\n"
	"^\tMatches the start of the filename\r\n"
	"$\tMatches the end of the filename\r\n"
	"( )\tDefines a marked subexpression\r\n"
	"\\1 - \\9\tMatches what the nth marked subexpression matched\r\n"
	"*\tMatches the preceding element zero or more times\r\n"
	"?\tMatches the preceding element zero or one times\r\n"
	"+\tMatches the preceding element one or more times\r\n"
	"*?\tLazily matches the preceding element zero or more times\r\n"
	"+?\tLazily matches the preceding element one or more times\r\n"
	"{x}\tMatches the preceding element x times\r\n"
	"{x,}\tMatches the preceding element x or more times\r\n"
	"{x,y}\tMatches the preceding element between x and y times\r\n"
	"\\\tEscape special character\r\n"
	"\\Q...\\E\tLiteral sequence ...\r\n"
	"\\a\tAlarm, that is, the BEL character (hex 07)\r\n"
	"\\cx\t\"Control-x\", where x is any ASCII character\r\n"
	"\\e\tEscape (hex 1B)\r\n"
	"\\f\tForm feed (hex 0C)\r\n"
	"\\n\tLinefeed (hex 0A)\r\n"
	"\\r\tCarriage return (hex 0D)\r\n"
	"\\t\tTab (hex 09)\r\n"
	"\\0dd\tCharacter with octal code 0dd\r\n"
	"\\ddd\tCharacter with octal code ddd, or back reference\r\n"
	"\\o{ddd..}\tCharacter with octal code ddd..\r\n"
	"\\xhh\tCharacter with hex code hh\r\n"
	"\\x{hhh..}\tCharacter with hex code hhh..\r\n"
	"\\d\tAny decimal digit\r\n"
	"\\D\tAny character that is not a decimal digit\r\n"
	"\\h\tAny horizontal white space character\r\n"
	"\\H\tAny character that is not a horizontal white space character\r\n"
	"\\s\tAny white space character\r\n"
	"\\S\tAny character that is not a white space character\r\n"
	"\\v\tAny vertical white space character\r\n"
	"\\V\tAny character that is not a vertical white space character\r\n"
	"\\w\tAny \"word\" character\r\n"
	"\\W\tAny \"non-word\" character\r\n"
	"\\p{xx}\tA character with the xx property\r\n"
	"\\P{xx}\tA character without the xx property\r\n"
	"\\X\tA Unicode extended grapheme cluster\r\n"
	"\\b\tMatches at a word boundary\r\n"
	"\\B\tMatches when not at a word boundary\r\n"
	"\\A\tMatches at the start of the subject\r\n"
	"\\Z\tMatches at the end of the subject also matches before a newline at the end of the subject\r\n"
	"\\z\tMatches only at the end of the subject\r\n"
	"\\G\tMatches at the first matching position in the subject\r\n"
	
HELP_SEARCH_SYNTAX_CAPTION = "Search Syntax - Everything"
	
HELP_SEARCH_SYNTAX_TEXT = "\r\n"
	"Operators:\r\n" 
	"\tspace\tAND\r\n"
	"\t|\tOR\r\n"
	"\t!\tNOT\r\n"
	"\t< >\tGrouping\r\n"
	"\t\" \"\tSearch for an exact phrase.\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Wildcards:\r\n"
	"\t*\tMatches zero or more characters.\r\n"
	"\t?\tMatches one character.\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Macros:\r\n"
	"\tquot:\tLiteral double quote (\")\r\n"
	"\tapos:\tLiteral apostrophe (')\r\n"
	"\tamp:\tLiteral ampersand (&)\r\n"
	"\tlt:\tLiteral less than (<)\r\n"
	"\tgt:\tLiteral greater than (>)\r\n"
	"\t#<n>:\tLiteral Unicode character <n> in decimal.\r\n"
	"\t#x<n>:\tLiteral Unicode character <n> in hexadecimal.\r\n"
	"\taudio:\tSearch for audio files.\r\n"
	"\tzip:\tSearch for compressed files.\r\n"
	"\tdoc:\tSearch for document files.\r\n"
	"\texe:\tSearch for executable files.\r\n"
	"\tpic:\tSearch for picture files.\r\n"
	"\tvideo:\tSearch for video files.\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Modifiers:\r\n"
	"\tascii:\tEnable fast ASCII case comparisons.\r\n"
	"\tcase:\tMatch case.\r\n"
	"\tdiacritics:\tMatch diacritical marks.\r\n"
	"\tfile:\tMatch files only.\r\n"
	"\tfolder:\tMatch folders only.\r\n"
	"\tnoascii:\tDisable fast ASCII case comparisons.\r\n"
	"\tnocase:\tDo not match case.\r\n"
	"\tnodiacritics:\tDo not match diacritical marks.\r\n"
	"\tnofileonly:\tDo not allow files only.\r\n"
	"\tnofolderonly:\tDo not allow folders only.\r\n"
	"\tnopath:\tDo not match path.\r\n"
	"\tnoregex:\tDisable regex.\r\n"
	"\tnowfn:\tDo not match the whole filename.\r\n"
	"\tnowholefilename:\tDo not match the whole filename.\r\n"
	"\tnowholeword:\tDo not match whole words only.\r\n"
	"\tnowildcards:\tDisable wildcards.\r\n"
	"\tnoww:\tDo not match whole words only.\r\n"
	"\tpath:\tMatch path and file name.\r\n"
	"\tregex:\tEnable regex.\r\n"
	"\tutf8:\tDisable fast ASCII case comparisons.\r\n"
	"\twfn:\tMatch the whole filename.\r\n"
	"\twholefilename:\tMatch the whole filename.\r\n"
	"\twholeword:\tMatch whole words only.\r\n"
	"\twildcards:\tEnable wildcards.\r\n"
	"\tww:\tMatch whole words only.\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Functions:\r\n"
	"\talbum:<text>\tSearch media for album meta data.\r\n"
	"\tansicontent:<text>\tSearch ANSI file content for text.\r\n"

	"Function Syntax:\r\n"
	"\tfunction:value\tEqual to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<=value\tLess than or equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<value\tLess than value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:=value\tEqual to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:>value\tGreater than value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:>=value\tGreater than or equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:start..end\tIs in the range of values from start to end.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:start-end\tIs in the range of values from start to end.\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Size Syntax:\r\n"
	"\tsize[kb|mb|gb]\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Size Constants:\r\n"
	"\tempty\r\n"
	"\ttiny\t0 KB < size <= 10 KB\r\n"
	"\tsmall\t10 KB < size <= 100 KB\r\n"
	"\tmedium\t100 KB < size <= 1 MB\r\n"
	"\tlarge\t1 MB < size <= 16 MB\r\n"
	"\thuge\t16 MB < size <= 128 MB\r\n"
	"\tgigantic\tsize > 128 MB\r\n"
	"\tunknown\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Date Syntax:\r\n"
	"\tyear\r\n"
	"\tmonth/year or year/month depending on locale settings\r\n"
	"\tday/month/year, month/day/year or year/month/day depending on locale settings\r\n"
	"\tYYYY[-MM[-DD[Thh[:mm[:ss[.sss]]]]]]\r\n"
	"\tYYYYMM[DD[Thh[mm[ss[.sss]]]]]\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"Date Constants:\r\n"
	"\ttoday\r\n"
	"\tyesterday\r\n"
	"\ttomorrow\r\n"
	"\t<last|past|prev|current|this|coming|next><year|month|week>\r\n"
	"\t<last|past|prev|coming|next><x><years|months|weeks|days|hours|minutes|mins|seconds|secs>\r\n"
	"\tjanuary|february|march|april|may|june|july|august|september|october|november|december\r\n"
	"\tjan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec\r\n"
	"\tsunday|monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday\r\n"
	"\tsun|mon|tue|wed|thu|fri|sat\r\n"
	"\tunknown\r\n"
	"\r\n"

	"\tA\tArchive\r\n"

// v2 of HELP_SEARCH_SYNTAX_TEXT
HELP_SEARCH_SYNTAX_TEXT2 = "\r\n"
	"Operators:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tspace\tAND\r\n"
	"\t|\tOR\r\n"
	"\t!\tNOT\r\n"
	"\t< >\tGrouping\r\n"
	"\t\" \"\tEscape operator characters.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Wildcard matching:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\t*\tMatches any character (except \\) zero or more times.\r\n"
	"\t**\tMatches any character zero or more times.\r\n"
	"\t?\tMatches any single character (except \\).\r\n"
	"\tThe whole filename is matched when using a wildcard.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Character entities:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\t&sp:\tLiteral space ( )\r\n"
	"\t&vert:\tLiteral vertical line (|)\r\n"
	"\t&excl:\tLiteral exclamation mark (!)\r\n"
	"\t&lt:\tLiteral less than (<)\r\n"
	"\t&gt:\tLiteral greater than (>)\r\n"
	"\t&quot:\tLiteral double quote (\")\r\n"
	"\t&#<n>:\tLiteral Unicode character <n> in decimal.\r\n"
	"\t&#x<n>:\tLiteral Unicode character <n> in hexadecimal.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Macros:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\taudio:\tSearch for audio files.\r\n"
	"\tzip:\tSearch for compressed files.\r\n"
	"\tdoc:\tSearch for document files.\r\n"
	"\texe:\tSearch for executable files.\r\n"
	"\timage:\tSearch for image files.\r\n"
	"\tvideo:\tSearch for video files.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Modifiers:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tbinary:\tMatch as a byte stream, \\\\ = \\ \\xff = hex byte.\r\n"
	"\tcase:\tMatch case.\r\n"
	"\tdiacritics:\tMatch diacritical marks.\r\n"
	"\tendwith:\tMatch the end of the filename or property.\r\n"
	"\tfile:\tMatch files only.\r\n"
	"\tfolder:\tMatch folders only.\r\n"
	"\thex:\tConvert double hex characters to bytes.\r\n"
	"\thighlight:\tHighlight the search term.\r\n"
	"\tignorepunc:\tIgnore punctuation in the filename or property.\r\n"
	"\tignorews:\tIgnore white space in the filename or property.\r\n"
	"\tlen:\tMatch the length of the filename or property in UTF-16 characters.\r\n"
	"\tfromdisk:\tSearch for properties and content from disk.\r\n"
	"\ttonumber:\tConvert text to a number for comparison.\r\n"
	"\tpath:\tMatch the full path.\r\n"
	"\tprefix:\tMatch the start of a word.\r\n"
	"\tregex:\tEnable regular expressions.\r\n"
	"\tstartwith:\tMatch the start of the filename or property.\r\n"
	"\tsuffix:\tMatch the end of a word.\r\n"
	"\ttostring:\tConvert property to the display string for comparison.\r\n"
	"\twhole:\tMatch the whole filename or property.\r\n"
	"\tww:\tMatch whole words only.\r\n"
	"\twildcards:\tEnable content wildcards.\r\n"
	"\tDisable a modifier with the no prefix.\r\n"
	"\tModifers can be combined and used with search functions.\r\n"
	"\tPrefix a modifier with ? to enable it globally.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"wildcards: search modifier syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\t*\tMatches any character zero or more times.\r\n"
	"\t?\tMatches any single character.\r\n"
	"\t#\tMatches any single digit (0-9).\r\n"
	"\t[ ]\tMatches any one of the characters specified in the set.\r\n"
	"\t[! ]\tMatches any one character that is not specified in the set.\r\n"
	"\t\\\tEscape the following character.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Functions:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\talbum:\tSearch for media files where the album property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tartist:\tSearch for media files where the artist property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tattrib:\tSearch for files and folders where the attributes include all the specified flags.\r\n"
	"\tbitdepth:\tSearch for media files where the bit depth property matches the specified number.\r\n"
	"\tchild:\tSearch for folders where the filename of a child contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tchild-count:\tSearch for folders where the number of subfolders and files matches the specified count.\r\n"
	"\tchild-file-count:\tSearch for folders where the number of files matches the specified count.\r\n"
	"\tchild-folder-count:\tSearch for folders where the number of subfolders matches the specified count.\r\n"
	"\tcomment:\tSearch for media files where the comment property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tcontent:\tSearch for files where the content contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tcount:\tLimit the number of results to the specified count.\r\n"
	"\tdc:\tSearch for files and folders where the date created matches the specified date.\r\n"
	"\tdepth:\tSearch for files and folders where the number of parents matches the specified count.\r\n"
	"\tdm:\tSearch for files and folders where the date modified matches the specified date.\r\n"
	"\tdupe:\tSearch for files and folders where the values of the specified property type are duplicated.\r\n"
	"\tempty:\tSearch for folders where the number of subfolders and files is zero.\r\n"
	"\text:\tSearch for files where the extension is in the specified semicolon delimited list.\r\n"
	"\tfilelist:\tSearch for files and folders where the filename is in the specified semicolon delimited list.\r\n"
	"\tfilelist-filename:\tSearch for files and folders where the filename of the owning file list contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tfrn:\tSearch for files and folders where the File Reference Number matches the specified number.\r\n"
	"\tgenre:\tSearch for media files where the genre property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\theight:\tSearch for media files where the height property matches the specified number in pixels.\r\n"
	"\tindex-type:\tSearch for files and folders where the index type property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\tlength:\tSearch for media files where the length property matches the specified duration.\r\n"
	"\tname:\tSearch for files and folders where the name part contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\torientation:\tSearch for media files where the aspect ratio property is landscape or portrait.\r\n"
	"\tparent:\tSearch for files and folders where the parent matches the specified path.\r\n"
	"\tpath-part:\tSearch for files and folders where the path part contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\troot:\tSearch for files and folders with no parent folder.\r\n"
	"\trun-count:\tSearch for files and folders where the run count property matches the specified number.\r\n"
	"\tsi:\tSearch the system index with the specified advanced query syntax.\r\n"
	"\tsize:\tSearch for files and folders where the size matches the specified number of bytes.\r\n"
	"\tstar-rating:\tSearch for media files where the rating property matches the specified value (1-5).\r\n"
	"\tstem:\tSearch for files and folders where the name without extension contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\ttag:\tSearch for media files where the tag property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\ttitle:\tSearch for media files where the title property contains the specified text.\r\n"
	"\ttrack:\tSearch for media files where the track property matches the specified number.\r\n"
	"\ttype:\tSearch for files and folders where the type matches the specified text.\r\n"
	"\twidth:\tSearch for media files where the width property matches the specified number in pixels.\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Function Syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tfunction:value\tEqual to value within the specified granularity.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<=value\tLess than or equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<value\tLess than value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:=value\tExactly equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:==value\tExactly equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:>value\tGreater than value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:>=value\tGreater than or equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:!=value\tNot equal to value.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:!value\tNot equal to value with specified granularity.\r\n"
	"\tfunction:start..end\tIs in the range of values from start to end (inclusive).\r\n"
	"\tfunction:start-end\tIs in the range of values from start to end (inclusive).\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<val1 val2>\tMatches val1 AND val2\r\n"
	"\tfunction:<val1 | val2>\tMatches val1 OR val2\r\n"
	"\tfunction:val1;val2\tMatches val1 OR val2\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Size Syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tsize[kb|mb|gb]\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Size Constants:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tempty\t0 bytes\r\n"
	"\ttiny\t0 KB < size <= 10 KB\r\n"
	"\tsmall\t10 KB < size <= 100 KB\r\n"
	"\tmedium\t100 KB < size <= 1 MB\r\n"
	"\tlarge\t1 MB < size <= 16 MB\r\n"
	"\thuge\t16 MB < size <= 128 MB\r\n"
	"\tgigantic\tsize > 128 MB\r\n"
	"\tunknown\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Duration Syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\t[[[DD:]HH:]MM:]SS[.sss]\r\n"
	"\t[<n><d|day|days>][<n><h|hour|hours>][<n><m|min|mins|minute|minutes>][<n><s|sec|secs|second|seconds>]\r\n"
	"\tP[n]Y[n]M[n]DT[n]H[n]M[n]S\r\n"
	"\tP[n]W\r\n"
	"\tPYYYYMMDDThhmmss\r\n"
	"\tP[YYYY]-[MM]-[DD]T[hh]:[mm]:[ss]\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Duration Constants:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tvery-short\tUnder 1 minute.\r\n"
	"\tshort\t1 - 5 minutes.\r\n"
	"\tmedium\t5 - 30 minutes.\r\n"
	"\tlong\t30 - 60 minutes.\r\n"
	"\tvery-long\tOver 60 minutes.\r\n"
	"\tunknown\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Date Syntax:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tyear\r\n"
	"\tmonth/year or year/month depending on locale settings\r\n"
	"\tday/month/year, month/day/year or year/month/day depending on locale settings\r\n"
	"\tYYYY[-MM[-DD[Thh[:mm[:ss[.sss]]]]]]\r\n"
	"\tYYYYMMDD[Thh[mm[ss[.sss]]]]]\r\n"
	"\tYYMMDD\r\n"
	"\tFILETIME (>99999999)\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Date Constants:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\ttoday\r\n"
	"\tyesterday\r\n"
	"\t<last|current|this|coming|next><year|month|week>\r\n"
	"\t<last|coming|next><x><years|months|weeks|days|hours|minutes|mins|seconds|secs>\r\n"
	"\tpast[x]<year[s]|month[s]|week[s]|day[s]|hour[s]|minute[s]|min[s]|second[s]|sec[s]>\r\n"
	"\t<prev|previous>[x]<year[s]|month[s]|week[s]>\r\n"
	"\tjanuary|february|march|april|may|june|july|august|september|october|november|december\r\n"
	"\tjan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec\r\n"
	"\tsunday|monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday\r\n"
	"\tsun|mon|tue|wed|thu|fri|sat\r\n"
	"\tmtd|ytd\r\n"
	"\tunknown\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Attribute Constants:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tA\tArchive\r\n"
	"\tC\tCompressed\r\n"
	"\tD\tDirectory\r\n"
	"\tE\tEncrypted\r\n"
	"\tH\tHidden\r\n"
	"\tI\tNot content indexed\r\n"
	"\tL\tReparse point\r\n"
	"\tM\tRecall on data access\r\n"
	"\tN\tNormal\r\n"
	"\tO\tOffline\r\n"
	"\tP\tPinned\r\n"
	"\tR\tRead only\r\n"
	"\tS\tSystem\r\n"
	"\tT\tTemporary\r\n"
	"\tU\tUnpinned\r\n"
	"\tV\tIntegrity stream\r\n"
	"\tX\tNo scrub data\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Filename parts:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tFull Path\tC:\\folder\\file.txt\r\n"
	"\tName\tfile.txt\r\n"
	"\tPath\tC:\\folder\r\n"
	"\tStem\tfile\r\n"
	"\tExtension\ttxt\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"Examples:\r\n"
	"\r\n"
	"\tc:\tSearch for files and folders on the C: drive.\r\n"
	"\td:|e:\tSearch for files and folders on the D: OR E: drive.\r\n"
	"\t!f:\tSearch for files and folders NOT on the F: drive.\r\n"
	"\t\\downloads\tSearch for files and folders in a Downloads folder.\r\n"
	"\t!\\appdata\tSearch for files and folders NOT in a appdata folder.\r\n"
	"\tc:\\windows\\\tSearch for files and folders in C:\\Windows.\r\n"
	"\t\"c:\\Program Files\\\"\tSearch for files and folders in C:\\Program Files.\r\n"
	"\tsize:>50mb\tSearch for files and folders where the size is larger than 50 MB.\r\n"
	"\tsize:10mb..50mb\tSearch for files and folders where the size is between 10 MB and 50 MB.\r\n"
	"\tsize:<1mb\tSearch for files and folders where the size is smaller than 1 MB.\r\n"
	"\tdm:today\tSearch for files and folders where the date modified is today.\r\n"
	"\tdm:>2022\tSearch for files and folders where the date modified is after 2022.\r\n"
	"\tdm:2021-07..2022-06\tSearch for files and folders where the date modified is between July 2021 and June 2022.\r\n"
	"\tdm:<2020\tSearch for files and folders where the date modified is before 2020.\r\n"
	"\t*.mp3\tSearch for mp3 files.\r\n"
	"\text:jpg;png\tSearch for files where the extension matches jpg or png.\r\n"
	"\tattrib:h\tSearch for files and folders where the attributes contain the hidden flag.\r\n"
	"\tlength:>1hour\tSearch for media files where the length is longer than 1 hour.\r\n"
	"\tlength:10mins..30mins\tSearch for media files where the length is between 10 minutes and 30 minutes.\r\n"
	"\tlength:<1min\tSearch for media files where the length is less than 1 minute.\r\n"
	"\tcontent:abc\tSearch for files where the content contains abc.\r\n"
	"\tcontent:<abc 123>\tSearch for files where the content contains abc AND 123.\r\n"
	"\tregex:content:^foo\tSearch for files where the content starts with foo.\r\n"
